# Azure Quest Polished Question Bank v5

Total: 600 rewritten scenario-style questions.

## SC-300

### Implement and manage user identities

#### sc300-d1-q01 (easy)

**Scenario:** FortisAid Healthcare

FortisAid Healthcare is working in a healthcare tenant with sensitive patient data. The security lead needs to verify a custom domain and present trusted sign-in branding. Which action best satisfies the requirement while following least privilege?

- A. add the DNS TXT record and configure company branding
- B. change the default tenant name only
- C. create a Conditional Access policy for the domain
- D. assign licenses before verification

**Answer:** A

**Explanation:** The best answer is to add the DNS TXT record and configure company branding. This directly addresses tenant setup and domain management, keeps permissions scoped, and matches the exam objective for Implement and manage user identities.

**Why the others are wrong:**
- B: This does not fully meet the tenant setup and domain management requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- C: This does not fully meet the tenant setup and domain management requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- D: This does not fully meet the tenant setup and domain management requirement or creates unnecessary risk.

#### sc300-d1-q02 (medium)

**Scenario:** ClearVault Finance

During a review at ClearVault Finance, auditors found a gap related to administrative units and delegated administration. You must fix it without adding unnecessary standing access. What should you do?

- A. make the team Global Administrators
- B. scope the role assignment to an administrative unit
- C. create a dynamic group only
- D. use a device compliance policy

**Answer:** B

**Explanation:** The best answer is to scope the role assignment to an administrative unit. This directly addresses administrative units and delegated administration, keeps permissions scoped, and matches the exam objective for Implement and manage user identities.

**Why the others are wrong:**
- A: This does not fully meet the administrative units and delegated administration requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- C: This does not fully meet the administrative units and delegated administration requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- D: This does not fully meet the administrative units and delegated administration requirement or creates unnecessary risk.

#### sc300-d1-q03 (medium)

**Scenario:** Helix x Pulse Networks

A change request at Helix x Pulse Networks says: "onboard many employees with consistent attributes and licenses." The solution must be auditable and aligned to Microsoft cloud security practices. Which option should you choose?

- A. manually create every account
- B. ask Microsoft Support to import the users
- C. use Microsoft Graph PowerShell or bulk CSV import with group-based licensing
- D. store passwords in a shared spreadsheet

**Answer:** C

**Explanation:** The best answer is to use Microsoft Graph PowerShell or bulk CSV import with group-based licensing. This directly addresses bulk user creation and attributes, keeps permissions scoped, and matches the exam objective for Implement and manage user identities.

**Why the others are wrong:**
- A: This does not fully meet the bulk user creation and attributes requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- B: This does not fully meet the bulk user creation and attributes requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- D: This does not fully meet the bulk user creation and attributes requirement or creates unnecessary risk.

#### sc300-d1-q04 (hard)

**Scenario:** Nexus Financial

Nexus Financial has a production issue involving dynamic groups and group lifecycle. The team wants the fastest secure remediation, not a temporary workaround. What is the best answer? The solution must minimize blast radius and preserve investigation evidence.

- A. use a static assigned group
- B. grant access directly to each user
- C. create a Conditional Access named location
- D. create a dynamic membership rule on the required attribute

**Answer:** D

**Explanation:** The best answer is to create a dynamic membership rule on the required attribute. This directly addresses dynamic groups and group lifecycle, keeps permissions scoped, and matches the exam objective for Implement and manage user identities. In exam scenarios, prefer controls that are enforceable, auditable, and least-privileged over broad access or manual process.

**Why the others are wrong:**
- A: This does not fully meet the dynamic groups and group lifecycle requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- B: This does not fully meet the dynamic groups and group lifecycle requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- C: This does not fully meet the dynamic groups and group lifecycle requirement or creates unnecessary risk.

#### sc300-d1-q05 (medium)

**Scenario:** FortisAid Healthcare

You are designing controls for FortisAid Healthcare. The requirement is to synchronize selected on-premises identities to Entra ID. Which implementation is the most appropriate?

- A. configure Microsoft Entra Connect Sync or Cloud Sync with filtering
- B. create cloud-only duplicates
- C. use B2B collaboration for employees
- D. enable PIM for every synced account

**Answer:** A

**Explanation:** The best answer is to configure Microsoft Entra Connect Sync or Cloud Sync with filtering. This directly addresses hybrid identity synchronization, keeps permissions scoped, and matches the exam objective for Implement and manage user identities.

**Why the others are wrong:**
- B: This does not fully meet the hybrid identity synchronization requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- C: This does not fully meet the hybrid identity synchronization requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- D: This does not fully meet the hybrid identity synchronization requirement or creates unnecessary risk.

#### sc300-d1-q06 (easy)

**Scenario:** ClearVault Finance

ClearVault Finance is working in a secure Azure landing zone. The security lead needs to collaborate with partner users while limiting their tenant access. Which action best satisfies the requirement while following least privilege?

- A. create permanent member accounts for all partners
- B. configure External Identities, cross-tenant access settings, and scoped app access
- C. disable guest access reviews
- D. share an administrator account

**Answer:** B

**Explanation:** The best answer is to configure External Identities, cross-tenant access settings, and scoped app access. This directly addresses external identities and B2B, keeps permissions scoped, and matches the exam objective for Implement and manage user identities.

**Why the others are wrong:**
- A: This does not fully meet the external identities and B2B requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- C: This does not fully meet the external identities and B2B requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- D: This does not fully meet the external identities and B2B requirement or creates unnecessary risk.

#### sc300-d1-q07 (medium)

**Scenario:** Helix x Pulse Networks

During a review at Helix x Pulse Networks, auditors found a gap related to tenant setup and domain management. You must fix it without adding unnecessary standing access. What should you do?

- A. change the default tenant name only
- B. create a Conditional Access policy for the domain
- C. add the DNS TXT record and configure company branding
- D. assign licenses before verification

**Answer:** C

**Explanation:** The best answer is to add the DNS TXT record and configure company branding. This directly addresses tenant setup and domain management, keeps permissions scoped, and matches the exam objective for Implement and manage user identities.

**Why the others are wrong:**

- D: This does not fully meet the tenant setup and domain management requirement or creates unnecessary risk.

#### sc300-d1-q08 (medium)

**Scenario:** Nexus Financial

A change request at Nexus Financial says: "delegate user administration for one department without tenant-wide rights." The solution must be auditable and aligned to Microsoft cloud security practices. Which option should you choose?

- A. make the team Global Administrators
- B. create a dynamic group only
- C. use a device compliance policy
- D. scope the role assignment to an administrative unit

**Answer:** D

**Explanation:** The best answer is to scope the role assignment to an administrative unit. This directly addresses administrative units and delegated administration, keeps permissions scoped, and matches the exam objective for Implement and manage user identities.

**Why the others are wrong:**
- A: This does not fully meet the administrative units and delegated administration requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- B: This does not fully meet the administrative units and delegated administration requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- C: This does not fully meet the administrative units and delegated administration requirement or creates unnecessary risk.

#### sc300-d1-q10 (medium)

**Scenario:** ClearVault Finance

You are designing controls for ClearVault Finance. The requirement is to automatically grant access based on user attributes. Which implementation is the most appropriate?

- A. use a static assigned group
- B. create a dynamic membership rule on the required attribute
- C. grant access directly to each user
- D. create a Conditional Access named location

**Answer:** B

**Explanation:** The best answer is to create a dynamic membership rule on the required attribute. This directly addresses dynamic groups and group lifecycle, keeps permissions scoped, and matches the exam objective for Implement and manage user identities.

**Why the others are wrong:**

A change request at FortisAid Healthcare says: "onboard many employees with consistent attributes and licenses." The solution must be auditable and aligned to Microsoft cloud security practices. Which option should you choose?

- A. use Microsoft Graph PowerShell or bulk CSV import with group-based licensing
- B. manually create every account
- C. ask Microsoft Support to import the users
- D. store passwords in a shared spreadsheet

**Answer:** A

**Explanation:** The best answer is to use Microsoft Graph PowerShell or bulk CSV import with group-based licensing. This directly addresses bulk user creation and attributes, keeps permissions scoped, and matches the exam objective for Implement and manage user identities.

**Why the others are wrong:**
- B: This does not fully meet the bulk user creation and attributes requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- C: This does not fully meet the bulk user creation and attributes requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- D: This does not fully meet the bulk user creation and attributes requirement or creates unnecessary risk.

#### sc300-d1-q34 (hard)

**Scenario:** ClearVault Finance

ClearVault Finance has a production issue involving dynamic groups and group lifecycle. The team wants the fastest secure remediation, not a temporary workaround. What is the best answer? The solution must minimize blast radius and preserve investigation evidence.

- A. use a static assigned group
- B. create a dynamic membership rule on the required attribute
- C. grant access directly to each user
- D. create a Conditional Access named location

**Answer:** B

**Explanation:** The best answer is to create a dynamic membership rule on the required attribute. This directly addresses dynamic groups and group lifecycle, keeps permissions scoped, and matches the exam objective for Implement and manage user identities. In exam scenarios, prefer controls that are enforceable, auditable, and least-privileged over broad access or manual process.

**Why the others are wrong:**
- A: This does not fully meet the dynamic groups and group lifecycle requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- C: This does not fully meet the dynamic groups and group lifecycle requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- D: This does not fully meet the dynamic groups and group lifecycle requirement or creates unnecessary risk.

#### sc300-d1-q35 (medium)

**Scenario:** Helix x Pulse Networks

You are designing controls for Helix x Pulse Networks. The requirement is to synchronize selected on-premises identities to Entra ID. Which implementation is the most appropriate?

- A. create cloud-only duplicates
- B. use B2B collaboration for employees
- C. configure Microsoft Entra Connect Sync or Cloud Sync with filtering
- D. enable PIM for every synced account

**Answer:** C

**Explanation:** The best answer is to configure Microsoft Entra Connect Sync or Cloud Sync with filtering. This directly addresses hybrid identity synchronization, keeps permissions scoped, and matches the exam objective for Implement and manage user identities.

**Why the others are wrong:**
- A: This does not fully meet the hybrid identity synchronization requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- B: This does not fully meet the hybrid identity synchronization requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- D: This does not fully meet the hybrid identity synchronization requirement or creates unnecessary risk.

- A. create permanent member accounts for all partners
- B. disable guest access reviews
- C. share an administrator account
- D. configure External Identities, cross-tenant access settings, and scoped app access

**Answer:** D

**Explanation:** The best answer is to configure External Identities, cross-tenant access settings, and scoped app access. This directly addresses external identities and B2B, keeps permissions scoped, and matches the exam objective for Implement and manage user identities.

### Implement authentication and access management

#### sc300-d2-q01 (easy)

**Scenario:** ClearVault Finance

ClearVault Finance is working in a secure Azure landing zone. The security lead needs to move users to stronger authentication methods. Which action best satisfies the requirement while following least privilege?

- A. turn on legacy per-user MFA only
- B. disable SSPR registration
- C. enable the authentication methods policy and registration campaign
- D. use password hash sync as MFA

**Answer:** C

**Explanation:** The best answer is to enable the authentication methods policy and registration campaign. This directly addresses authentication methods and MFA, keeps permissions scoped, and matches the exam objective for Implement authentication and access management.

**Why the others are wrong:**
- A: This does not fully meet the authentication methods and MFA requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- B: This does not fully meet the authentication methods and MFA requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- D: This does not fully meet the authentication methods and MFA requirement or creates unnecessary risk.

#### sc300-d2-q02 (medium)

**Scenario:** Helix x Pulse Networks

During a review at Helix x Pulse Networks, auditors found a gap related to Temporary Access Pass onboarding. You must fix it without adding unnecessary standing access. What should you do?

- A. email the user's password
- B. make the account exempt from MFA forever
- C. create a guest account instead
- D. issue a time-limited Temporary Access Pass

**Answer:** D

**Explanation:** The best answer is to issue a time-limited Temporary Access Pass. This directly addresses Temporary Access Pass onboarding, keeps permissions scoped, and matches the exam objective for Implement authentication and access management.

**Why the others are wrong:**
- A: This does not fully meet the Temporary Access Pass onboarding requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- B: This does not fully meet the Temporary Access Pass onboarding requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- C: This does not fully meet the Temporary Access Pass onboarding requirement or creates unnecessary risk.

#### sc300-d2-q03 (medium)

**Scenario:** Nexus Financial

A change request at Nexus Financial says: "require strong controls without locking out emergency accounts." The solution must be auditable and aligned to Microsoft cloud security practices. Which option should you choose?

- A. create a Conditional Access policy with exclusions for break-glass accounts
- B. target all users including break-glass
- C. use a storage firewall
- D. assign Global Administrator permanently

**Answer:** A

**Explanation:** The best answer is to create a Conditional Access policy with exclusions for break-glass accounts. This directly addresses Conditional Access design, keeps permissions scoped, and matches the exam objective for Implement authentication and access management.

**Why the others are wrong:**
- B: This does not fully meet the Conditional Access design requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- C: This does not fully meet the Conditional Access design requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- D: This does not fully meet the Conditional Access design requirement or creates unnecessary risk.

#### sc300-d2-q04 (hard)

**Scenario:** FortisAid Healthcare

FortisAid Healthcare has a production issue involving Identity Protection risk policies. The team wants the fastest secure remediation, not a temporary workaround. What is the best answer? The solution must minimize blast radius and preserve investigation evidence.

- A. use only audit logs
- B. configure user risk and sign-in risk policies with remediation controls
- C. disable sign-in logs
- D. create an access package

**Answer:** B

**Explanation:** The best answer is to configure user risk and sign-in risk policies with remediation controls. This directly addresses Identity Protection risk policies, keeps permissions scoped, and matches the exam objective for Implement authentication and access management. In exam scenarios, prefer controls that are enforceable, auditable, and least-privileged over broad access or manual process.

**Why the others are wrong:**
- A: This does not fully meet the Identity Protection risk policies requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- C: This does not fully meet the Identity Protection risk policies requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- D: This does not fully meet the Identity Protection risk policies requirement or creates unnecessary risk.

#### sc300-d2-q05 (medium)

**Scenario:** ClearVault Finance

You are designing controls for ClearVault Finance. The requirement is to block clients that cannot satisfy modern authentication controls. Which implementation is the most appropriate?

- A. block all trusted locations
- B. delete the users using old clients
- C. use Conditional Access client app conditions or authentication policy controls
- D. turn off company branding

**Answer:** C

**Explanation:** The best answer is to use Conditional Access client app conditions or authentication policy controls. This directly addresses legacy authentication blocking, keeps permissions scoped, and matches the exam objective for Implement authentication and access management.

**Why the others are wrong:**
- A: This does not fully meet the legacy authentication blocking requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- B: This does not fully meet the legacy authentication blocking requirement or creates unnecessary risk.

#### sc300-d2-q06 (easy)

**Scenario:** Helix x Pulse Networks

Helix x Pulse Networks is working in a post-acquisition identity consolidation. The security lead needs to respond quickly when user risk or account status changes. Which action best satisfies the requirement while following least privilege?

- A. increase token lifetime
- B. disable session controls
- C. use a static group only
- D. use CAE-capable sessions and supported Conditional Access controls

**Answer:** D

**Explanation:** The best answer is to use CAE-capable sessions and supported Conditional Access controls. This directly addresses Continuous Access Evaluation, keeps permissions scoped, and matches the exam objective for Implement authentication and access management.

**Why the others are wrong:**
- A: This does not fully meet the Continuous Access Evaluation requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- B: This does not fully meet the Continuous Access Evaluation requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- C: This does not fully meet the Continuous Access Evaluation requirement or creates unnecessary risk.

- B: This does not fully meet the authentication methods and MFA requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- C: This does not fully meet the authentication methods and MFA requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- D: This does not fully meet the authentication methods and MFA requirement or creates unnecessary risk.

#### sc300-d2-q16 (easy)

**Scenario:** FortisAid Healthcare

FortisAid Healthcare is working in a healthcare tenant with sensitive patient data. The security lead needs to let a new hire register passwordless methods without a phone yet. Which action best satisfies the requirement while following least privilege?

- A. email the user's password
- B. issue a time-limited Temporary Access Pass
- C. make the account exempt from MFA forever
- D. create a guest account instead

**Answer:** B

**Explanation:** The best answer is to issue a time-limited Temporary Access Pass. This directly addresses Temporary Access Pass onboarding, keeps permissions scoped, and matches the exam objective for Implement authentication and access management.

**Why the others are wrong:**

- C: This does not fully meet the Temporary Access Pass onboarding requirement or creates unnecessary risk.

#### sc300-d2-q17 (medium)

**Scenario:** ClearVault Finance

During a review at ClearVault Finance, auditors found a gap related to Conditional Access design. You must fix it without adding unnecessary standing access. What should you do?

- A. target all users including break-glass
- B. use a storage firewall
- C. create a Conditional Access policy with exclusions for break-glass accounts
- D. assign Global Administrator permanently

**Answer:** C

**Explanation:** The best answer is to create a Conditional Access policy with exclusions for break-glass accounts. This directly addresses Conditional Access design, keeps permissions scoped, and matches the exam objective for Implement authentication and access management.

**Why the others are wrong:**
- A: This does not fully meet the Conditional Access design requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- B: This does not fully meet the Conditional Access design requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- D: This does not fully meet the Conditional Access design requirement or creates unnecessary risk.

#### sc300-d2-q18 (medium)

**Scenario:** Helix x Pulse Networks

A change request at Helix x Pulse Networks says: "respond automatically to risky users and risky sign-ins." The solution must be auditable and aligned to Microsoft cloud security practices. Which option should you choose?

- A. use only audit logs
- B. disable sign-in logs
- C. create an access package
- D. configure user risk and sign-in risk policies with remediation controls

**Answer:** D

**Explanation:** The best answer is to configure user risk and sign-in risk policies with remediation controls. This directly addresses Identity Protection risk policies, keeps permissions scoped, and matches the exam objective for Implement authentication and access management.

**Why the others are wrong:**
- A: This does not fully meet the Identity Protection risk policies requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- B: This does not fully meet the Identity Protection risk policies requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- C: This does not fully meet the Identity Protection risk policies requirement or creates unnecessary risk.

#### sc300-d2-q19 (hard)

**Scenario:** Nexus Financial

Nexus Financial has a production issue involving legacy authentication blocking. The team wants the fastest secure remediation, not a temporary workaround. What is the best answer? The solution must minimize blast radius and preserve investigation evidence.

- A. use Conditional Access client app conditions or authentication policy controls
- B. block all trusted locations
- C. delete the users using old clients
- D. turn off company branding

**Answer:** A

**Explanation:** The best answer is to use Conditional Access client app conditions or authentication policy controls. This directly addresses legacy authentication blocking, keeps permissions scoped, and matches the exam objective for Implement authentication and access management. In exam scenarios, prefer controls that are enforceable, auditable, and least-privileged over broad access or manual process.

**Why the others are wrong:**
- B: This does not fully meet the legacy authentication blocking requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- C: This does not fully meet the legacy authentication blocking requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- D: This does not fully meet the legacy authentication blocking requirement or creates unnecessary risk.

#### sc300-d2-q20 (medium)

**Scenario:** FortisAid Healthcare

You are designing controls for FortisAid Healthcare. The requirement is to respond quickly when user risk or account status changes. Which implementation is the most appropriate?

- A. increase token lifetime
- B. use CAE-capable sessions and supported Conditional Access controls
- C. disable session controls
- D. use a static group only

**Answer:** B

**Explanation:** The best answer is to use CAE-capable sessions and supported Conditional Access controls. This directly addresses Continuous Access Evaluation, keeps permissions scoped, and matches the exam objective for Implement authentication and access management.

**Why the others are wrong:**
- A: This does not fully meet the Continuous Access Evaluation requirement or creates unnecessary risk.

- D: This does not fully meet the Continuous Access Evaluation requirement or creates unnecessary risk.

#### sc300-d2-q49 (hard)

**Scenario:** ClearVault Finance

ClearVault Finance has a production issue involving Global Secure Access. The team wants the fastest secure remediation, not a temporary workaround. What is the best answer? The solution must minimize blast radius and preserve investigation evidence.

- A. publish the app with a public IP only
- B. bypass Conditional Access
- C. configure the appropriate Global Secure Access traffic profile and client
- D. use storage SAS tokens

**Answer:** C

**Explanation:** The best answer is to configure the appropriate Global Secure Access traffic profile and client. This directly addresses Global Secure Access, keeps permissions scoped, and matches the exam objective for Implement authentication and access management. In exam scenarios, prefer controls that are enforceable, auditable, and least-privileged over broad access or manual process.

**Why the others are wrong:**
- A: This does not fully meet the Global Secure Access requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- B: This does not fully meet the Global Secure Access requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- D: This does not fully meet the Global Secure Access requirement or creates unnecessary risk.

#### sc300-d2-q50 (medium)

**Scenario:** Helix x Pulse Networks

- A. turn on legacy per-user MFA only
- B. disable SSPR registration
- C. use password hash sync as MFA
- D. enable the authentication methods policy and registration campaign

**Answer:** D

- B: This does not fully meet the authentication methods and MFA requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- C: This does not fully meet the authentication methods and MFA requirement or creates unnecessary risk.

### Plan and implement workload identities

#### sc300-d3-q01 (easy)

**Scenario:** Helix x Pulse Networks

Helix x Pulse Networks is working in a post-acquisition identity consolidation. The security lead needs to allow a custom app to sign in users securely. Which action best satisfies the requirement while following least privilege?

- A. register the app and configure platform, redirect URI, and permissions
- B. create a normal user account for the app
- C. store an admin password in code
- D. use a dynamic group as the app identity

**Answer:** A

**Explanation:** The best answer is to register the app and configure platform, redirect URI, and permissions. This directly addresses app registrations and redirect URIs, keeps permissions scoped, and matches the exam objective for Plan and implement workload identities.

**Why the others are wrong:**
- B: This does not fully meet the app registrations and redirect URIs requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- C: This does not fully meet the app registrations and redirect URIs requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- D: This does not fully meet the app registrations and redirect URIs requirement or creates unnecessary risk.

#### sc300-d3-q02 (medium)

**Scenario:** Nexus Financial

During a review at Nexus Financial, auditors found a gap related to API permissions and consent. You must fix it without adding unnecessary standing access. What should you do?

- A. grant Directory.ReadWrite.All by default
- B. grant only required delegated or application API permissions and require admin consent when appropriate
- C. allow all users to consent to high-risk apps
- D. use a Conditional Access location only

**Answer:** B

**Explanation:** The best answer is to grant only required delegated or application API permissions and require admin consent when appropriate. This directly addresses API permissions and consent, keeps permissions scoped, and matches the exam objective for Plan and implement workload identities.

**Why the others are wrong:**
- A: This does not fully meet the API permissions and consent requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- C: This does not fully meet the API permissions and consent requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- D: This does not fully meet the API permissions and consent requirement or creates unnecessary risk.

- A. create a storage account key
- B. use Azure Bastion
- C. configure the enterprise application with SAML or OIDC SSO
- D. create local accounts in the SaaS app only

FortisAid Healthcare is working in a healthcare tenant with sensitive patient data. The security lead needs to allow a custom app to sign in users securely. Which action best satisfies the requirement while following least privilege?

- A. create a normal user account for the app
- B. store an admin password in code
- C. register the app and configure platform, redirect URI, and permissions
- D. use a dynamic group as the app identity

**Answer:** C

**Explanation:** The best answer is to register the app and configure platform, redirect URI, and permissions. This directly addresses app registrations and redirect URIs, keeps permissions scoped, and matches the exam objective for Plan and implement workload identities.

**Why the others are wrong:**
- A: This does not fully meet the app registrations and redirect URIs requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- B: This does not fully meet the app registrations and redirect URIs requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- D: This does not fully meet the app registrations and redirect URIs requirement or creates unnecessary risk.

#### sc300-d3-q32 (medium)

**Scenario:** ClearVault Finance

During a review at ClearVault Finance, auditors found a gap related to API permissions and consent. You must fix it without adding unnecessary standing access. What should you do?

- A. grant Directory.ReadWrite.All by default
- B. allow all users to consent to high-risk apps
- C. use a Conditional Access location only
- D. grant only required delegated or application API permissions and require admin consent when appropriate

**Answer:** D

**Explanation:** The best answer is to grant only required delegated or application API permissions and require admin consent when appropriate. This directly addresses API permissions and consent, keeps permissions scoped, and matches the exam objective for Plan and implement workload identities.

**Why the others are wrong:**
- A: This does not fully meet the API permissions and consent requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- B: This does not fully meet the API permissions and consent requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- C: This does not fully meet the API permissions and consent requirement or creates unnecessary risk.

#### sc300-d3-q33 (medium)

**Scenario:** Helix x Pulse Networks

A change request at Helix x Pulse Networks says: "configure a third-party SaaS app for centralized sign-in." The solution must be auditable and aligned to Microsoft cloud security practices. Which option should you choose?

- A. configure the enterprise application with SAML or OIDC SSO
- B. create a storage account key
- C. use Azure Bastion
- D. create local accounts in the SaaS app only

**Answer:** A

**Explanation:** The best answer is to configure the enterprise application with SAML or OIDC SSO. This directly addresses enterprise applications and SSO, keeps permissions scoped, and matches the exam objective for Plan and implement workload identities.

**Why the others are wrong:**
- B: This does not fully meet the enterprise applications and SSO requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- C: This does not fully meet the enterprise applications and SSO requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- D: This does not fully meet the enterprise applications and SSO requirement or creates unnecessary risk.

#### sc300-d3-q34 (hard)

**Scenario:** Nexus Financial

Nexus Financial has a production issue involving managed identities. The team wants the fastest secure remediation, not a temporary workaround. What is the best answer? The solution must minimize blast radius and preserve investigation evidence.

- A. hardcode a client secret
- B. enable a managed identity and assign the minimum required RBAC role or vault permission
- C. grant Owner on the subscription
- D. use a personal administrator account

**Answer:** B

**Explanation:** The best answer is to enable a managed identity and assign the minimum required RBAC role or vault permission. This directly addresses managed identities, keeps permissions scoped, and matches the exam objective for Plan and implement workload identities. In exam scenarios, prefer controls that are enforceable, auditable, and least-privileged over broad access or manual process.

**Why the others are wrong:**
- A: This does not fully meet the managed identities requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- C: This does not fully meet the managed identities requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- D: This does not fully meet the managed identities requirement or creates unnecessary risk.

#### sc300-d3-q35 (medium)

**Scenario:** FortisAid Healthcare

You are designing controls for FortisAid Healthcare. The requirement is to secure automation used by deployment pipelines. Which implementation is the most appropriate?

- A. reuse a human admin account
- B. assign permanent Global Administrator
- C. use a service principal with scoped RBAC and certificate or federated credential
- D. store secrets in the repo

**Answer:** C

**Explanation:** The best answer is to use a service principal with scoped RBAC and certificate or federated credential. This directly addresses service principals, keeps permissions scoped, and matches the exam objective for Plan and implement workload identities.

- D. review workload identity sign-in logs and apply workload identity protections

### Plan and automate identity governance

#### sc300-d4-q01 (easy)

**Scenario:** Nexus Financial

Nexus Financial is working in a regulated finance environment. The security lead needs to replace standing admin rights with just-in-time access. Which action best satisfies the requirement while following least privilege?

- A. make admins permanently active
- B. use a distribution list
- C. configure PIM eligible assignments with approval, MFA, justification, and duration
- D. disable activation alerts

**Answer:** C

**Explanation:** The best answer is to configure PIM eligible assignments with approval, MFA, justification, and duration. This directly addresses Privileged Identity Management, keeps permissions scoped, and matches the exam objective for Plan and automate identity governance.

**Why the others are wrong:**
- A: This does not fully meet the Privileged Identity Management requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- B: This does not fully meet the Privileged Identity Management requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- D: This does not fully meet the Privileged Identity Management requirement or creates unnecessary risk.

#### sc300-d4-q02 (medium)

**Scenario:** FortisAid Healthcare

During a review at FortisAid Healthcare, auditors found a gap related to access reviews. You must fix it without adding unnecessary standing access. What should you do?

- A. export a CSV once a year only
- B. delete all guest users immediately
- C. use a named location
- D. create recurring access reviews with auto-apply decisions where appropriate

**Answer:** D

**Explanation:** The best answer is to create recurring access reviews with auto-apply decisions where appropriate. This directly addresses access reviews, keeps permissions scoped, and matches the exam objective for Plan and automate identity governance.

**Why the others are wrong:**
- A: This does not fully meet the access reviews requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- B: This does not fully meet the access reviews requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- C: This does not fully meet the access reviews requirement or creates unnecessary risk.

#### sc300-d4-q03 (medium)

**Scenario:** ClearVault Finance

A change request at ClearVault Finance says: "package access for contractors with approval and expiration." The solution must be auditable and aligned to Microsoft cloud security practices. Which option should you choose?

- A. create an access package in a catalog with request policy, approvers, and lifecycle settings
- B. directly assign every permission
- C. share an admin account
- D. disable guest expiration

**Answer:** A

**Explanation:** The best answer is to create an access package in a catalog with request policy, approvers, and lifecycle settings. This directly addresses entitlement management, keeps permissions scoped, and matches the exam objective for Plan and automate identity governance.

**Why the others are wrong:**
- B: This does not fully meet the entitlement management requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- C: This does not fully meet the entitlement management requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- D: This does not fully meet the entitlement management requirement or creates unnecessary risk.

#### sc300-d4-q04 (hard)

**Scenario:** Helix x Pulse Networks

Helix x Pulse Networks has a production issue involving Lifecycle Workflows. The team wants the fastest secure remediation, not a temporary workaround. What is the best answer? The solution must minimize blast radius and preserve investigation evidence.

- A. handle every change manually
- B. configure Lifecycle Workflows with triggers and tasks such as TAP, license removal, and account disablement
- C. use Sentinel analytics rules for onboarding
- D. create a storage firewall

**Answer:** B

**Explanation:** The best answer is to configure Lifecycle Workflows with triggers and tasks such as TAP, license removal, and account disablement. This directly addresses Lifecycle Workflows, keeps permissions scoped, and matches the exam objective for Plan and automate identity governance. In exam scenarios, prefer controls that are enforceable, auditable, and least-privileged over broad access or manual process.

**Why the others are wrong:**
- A: This does not fully meet the Lifecycle Workflows requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- C: This does not fully meet the Lifecycle Workflows requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- D: This does not fully meet the Lifecycle Workflows requirement or creates unnecessary risk.

- A. put sensitive attributes in displayName
- B. use ungoverned notes fields
- C. define and assign custom security attributes with delegated attribute roles
- D. make all users attribute administrators

**Explanation:** The best answer is to create an access package in a catalog with request policy, approvers, and lifecycle settings. This directly addresses entitlement management, keeps permissions scoped, and matches the exam objective for Plan and automate identity governance.

**Why the others are wrong:**
- A: This does not fully meet the entitlement management requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- B: This does not fully meet the entitlement management requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- D: This does not fully meet the entitlement management requirement or creates unnecessary risk.

#### sc300-d4-q14 (hard)

**Scenario:** FortisAid Healthcare

FortisAid Healthcare has a production issue involving Lifecycle Workflows. The team wants the fastest secure remediation, not a temporary workaround. What is the best answer? The solution must minimize blast radius and preserve investigation evidence.

- A. handle every change manually
- B. use Sentinel analytics rules for onboarding
- C. create a storage firewall
- D. configure Lifecycle Workflows with triggers and tasks such as TAP, license removal, and account disablement

**Answer:** D

**Explanation:** The best answer is to configure Lifecycle Workflows with triggers and tasks such as TAP, license removal, and account disablement. This directly addresses Lifecycle Workflows, keeps permissions scoped, and matches the exam objective for Plan and automate identity governance. In exam scenarios, prefer controls that are enforceable, auditable, and least-privileged over broad access or manual process.

**Why the others are wrong:**
- A: This does not fully meet the Lifecycle Workflows requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- B: This does not fully meet the Lifecycle Workflows requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- C: This does not fully meet the Lifecycle Workflows requirement or creates unnecessary risk.

FortisAid Healthcare is working in a healthcare tenant with sensitive patient data. The security lead needs to replace standing admin rights with just-in-time access. Which action best satisfies the requirement while following least privilege?

- A. make admins permanently active
- B. use a distribution list
- C. disable activation alerts
- D. configure PIM eligible assignments with approval, MFA, justification, and duration

**Answer:** D

**Explanation:** The best answer is to configure PIM eligible assignments with approval, MFA, justification, and duration. This directly addresses Privileged Identity Management, keeps permissions scoped, and matches the exam objective for Plan and automate identity governance.

**Why the others are wrong:**
- A: This does not fully meet the Privileged Identity Management requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- B: This does not fully meet the Privileged Identity Management requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- C: This does not fully meet the Privileged Identity Management requirement or creates unnecessary risk.

- B. export a CSV once a year only
- C. delete all guest users immediately

#### sc300-d4-q48 (medium)

- A. directly assign every permission
- B. create an access package in a catalog with request policy, approvers, and lifecycle settings
- C. share an admin account
- D. disable guest expiration

#### sc300-d4-q49 (hard)

**Scenario:** Nexus Financial

Nexus Financial has a production issue involving Lifecycle Workflows. The team wants the fastest secure remediation, not a temporary workaround. What is the best answer? The solution must minimize blast radius and preserve investigation evidence.

- A. handle every change manually
- B. use Sentinel analytics rules for onboarding
- C. configure Lifecycle Workflows with triggers and tasks such as TAP, license removal, and account disablement
- D. create a storage firewall

**Answer:** C

**Explanation:** The best answer is to configure Lifecycle Workflows with triggers and tasks such as TAP, license removal, and account disablement. This directly addresses Lifecycle Workflows, keeps permissions scoped, and matches the exam objective for Plan and automate identity governance. In exam scenarios, prefer controls that are enforceable, auditable, and least-privileged over broad access or manual process.

**Why the others are wrong:**
- A: This does not fully meet the Lifecycle Workflows requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- B: This does not fully meet the Lifecycle Workflows requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- D: This does not fully meet the Lifecycle Workflows requirement or creates unnecessary risk.

- B. use ungoverned notes fields

## AZ-500

### Secure identity and access

#### az500-d1-q01 (easy)

**Scenario:** FortisAid Healthcare

FortisAid Healthcare is working in a healthcare tenant with sensitive patient data. The security lead needs to grant operators access to one resource group only. Which action best satisfies the requirement while following least privilege?

- A. assign the least privileged Azure RBAC role at the resource group scope
- B. assign Owner at subscription scope
- C. make them Global Administrators
- D. share a deployment account

**Answer:** A

**Explanation:** The best answer is to assign the least privileged Azure RBAC role at the resource group scope. This directly addresses Azure RBAC and least privilege, keeps permissions scoped, and matches the exam objective for Secure identity and access.

**Why the others are wrong:**
- B: This does not fully meet the Azure RBAC and least privilege requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- C: This does not fully meet the Azure RBAC and least privilege requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- D: This does not fully meet the Azure RBAC and least privilege requirement or creates unnecessary risk.

#### az500-d1-q02 (medium)

**Scenario:** ClearVault Finance

- A. use permanent Contributor assignments
- B. configure PIM for Azure resources with eligible assignments and activation controls
- C. use NSGs to control admin roles
- D. disable audit logs

**Answer:** B

**Explanation:** The best answer is to configure PIM for Azure resources with eligible assignments and activation controls. This directly addresses PIM for Azure resources, keeps permissions scoped, and matches the exam objective for Secure identity and access.

**Why the others are wrong:**
- A: This does not fully meet the PIM for Azure resources requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- C: This does not fully meet the PIM for Azure resources requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- D: This does not fully meet the PIM for Azure resources requirement or creates unnecessary risk.

#### az500-d1-q03 (medium)

**Scenario:** Helix x Pulse Networks

A change request at Helix x Pulse Networks says: "remove hardcoded secrets from an app." The solution must be auditable and aligned to Microsoft cloud security practices. Which option should you choose?

- A. store the secret in app settings in plain text
- B. use a user password
- C. enable managed identity and authorize it to the required Key Vault secret
- D. grant Owner to the app

**Answer:** C

**Explanation:** The best answer is to enable managed identity and authorize it to the required Key Vault secret. This directly addresses managed identities and Key Vault, keeps permissions scoped, and matches the exam objective for Secure identity and access.

**Why the others are wrong:**
- A: This does not fully meet the managed identities and Key Vault requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- B: This does not fully meet the managed identities and Key Vault requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- D: This does not fully meet the managed identities and Key Vault requirement or creates unnecessary risk.

- A. allow all users to consent to any permission
- B. disable app registrations entirely
- C. use a storage firewall
- D. configure admin consent workflow and app consent policies

**Answer:** D

**Explanation:** The best answer is to configure admin consent workflow and app consent policies. This directly addresses application consent governance, keeps permissions scoped, and matches the exam objective for Secure identity and access. In exam scenarios, prefer controls that are enforceable, auditable, and least-privileged over broad access or manual process.

FortisAid Healthcare has a production issue involving application consent governance. The team wants the fastest secure remediation, not a temporary workaround. What is the best answer? The solution must minimize blast radius and preserve investigation evidence.

- A. configure admin consent workflow and app consent policies
- B. allow all users to consent to any permission
- C. disable app registrations entirely
- D. use a storage firewall

**Answer:** A

**Explanation:** The best answer is to configure admin consent workflow and app consent policies. This directly addresses application consent governance, keeps permissions scoped, and matches the exam objective for Secure identity and access. In exam scenarios, prefer controls that are enforceable, auditable, and least-privileged over broad access or manual process.

**Why the others are wrong:**
- B: This does not fully meet the application consent governance requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- C: This does not fully meet the application consent governance requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- D: This does not fully meet the application consent governance requirement or creates unnecessary risk.

#### az500-d1-q30 (medium)

- A. target only Exchange Online
- B. target Microsoft Azure Management with Conditional Access
- C. use a route table
- D. enable soft delete

**Answer:** B

**Explanation:** The best answer is to target Microsoft Azure Management with Conditional Access. This directly addresses Conditional Access for Azure management, keeps permissions scoped, and matches the exam objective for Secure identity and access.

- B. make them Global Administrators
- C. assign the least privileged Azure RBAC role at the resource group scope

### Secure networking

#### az500-d2-q01 (easy)

**Scenario:** ClearVault Finance

ClearVault Finance is working in a secure Azure landing zone. The security lead needs to allow web traffic to app servers while blocking direct database access. Which action best satisfies the requirement while following least privilege?

- A. open all inbound traffic
- B. use public IPs for databases
- C. create NSG rules using ASGs for source and destination tiers
- D. assign Owner to the subnet

**Answer:** C

**Explanation:** The best answer is to create NSG rules using ASGs for source and destination tiers. This directly addresses NSGs and ASGs, keeps permissions scoped, and matches the exam objective for Secure networking.

**Why the others are wrong:**
- A: This does not fully meet the NSGs and ASGs requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- B: This does not fully meet the NSGs and ASGs requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- D: This does not fully meet the NSGs and ASGs requirement or creates unnecessary risk.

#### az500-d2-q02 (medium)

**Scenario:** Helix x Pulse Networks

During a review at Helix x Pulse Networks, auditors found a gap related to Private Endpoints and Private Link. You must fix it without adding unnecessary standing access. What should you do?

- A. allow public network access from all networks
- B. use only an NSG on the client subnet
- C. share storage keys
- D. create Private Endpoints with private DNS integration

**Answer:** D

**Explanation:** The best answer is to create Private Endpoints with private DNS integration. This directly addresses Private Endpoints and Private Link, keeps permissions scoped, and matches the exam objective for Secure networking.

**Why the others are wrong:**
- A: This does not fully meet the Private Endpoints and Private Link requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- B: This does not fully meet the Private Endpoints and Private Link requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- C: This does not fully meet the Private Endpoints and Private Link requirement or creates unnecessary risk.

#### az500-d2-q03 (medium)

**Scenario:** Nexus Financial

A change request at Nexus Financial says: "centralize outbound filtering for hub-spoke networks." The solution must be auditable and aligned to Microsoft cloud security practices. Which option should you choose?

- A. route traffic through Azure Firewall and manage rules with firewall policy
- B. place NSGs only on every NIC
- C. disable UDRs
- D. use a public load balancer for egress control

**Answer:** A

**Explanation:** The best answer is to route traffic through Azure Firewall and manage rules with firewall policy. This directly addresses Azure Firewall and firewall policies, keeps permissions scoped, and matches the exam objective for Secure networking.

**Why the others are wrong:**
- B: This does not fully meet the Azure Firewall and firewall policies requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- C: This does not fully meet the Azure Firewall and firewall policies requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- D: This does not fully meet the Azure Firewall and firewall policies requirement or creates unnecessary risk.

#### az500-d2-q04 (hard)

- A. use a storage firewall
- B. enable WAF on Application Gateway or Azure Front Door with managed rules
- C. use only PIM
- D. turn off TLS inspection everywhere

**Answer:** B

**Explanation:** The best answer is to enable WAF on Application Gateway or Azure Front Door with managed rules. This directly addresses Web Application Firewall, keeps permissions scoped, and matches the exam objective for Secure networking. In exam scenarios, prefer controls that are enforceable, auditable, and least-privileged over broad access or manual process.

**Why the others are wrong:**

**Scenario:** FortisAid Healthcare

During a review at FortisAid Healthcare, auditors found a gap related to Network Watcher diagnostics. You must fix it without adding unnecessary standing access. What should you do?

- A. review company branding
- B. use Network Watcher IP flow verify, effective security rules, and connection troubleshoot
- C. use SSPR reports
- D. create a new tenant

**Answer:** B

**Explanation:** The best answer is to use Network Watcher IP flow verify, effective security rules, and connection troubleshoot. This directly addresses Network Watcher diagnostics, keeps permissions scoped, and matches the exam objective for Secure networking.

**Why the others are wrong:**
- A: This does not fully meet the Network Watcher diagnostics requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- C: This does not fully meet the Network Watcher diagnostics requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- D: This does not fully meet the Network Watcher diagnostics requirement or creates unnecessary risk.

#### az500-d2-q13 (medium)

**Scenario:** ClearVault Finance

A change request at ClearVault Finance says: "allow web traffic to app servers while blocking direct database access." The solution must be auditable and aligned to Microsoft cloud security practices. Which option should you choose?

- A. open all inbound traffic
- B. use public IPs for databases
- C. create NSG rules using ASGs for source and destination tiers
- D. assign Owner to the subnet

**Answer:** C

**Explanation:** The best answer is to create NSG rules using ASGs for source and destination tiers. This directly addresses NSGs and ASGs, keeps permissions scoped, and matches the exam objective for Secure networking.

**Why the others are wrong:**
- A: This does not fully meet the NSGs and ASGs requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- B: This does not fully meet the NSGs and ASGs requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- D: This does not fully meet the NSGs and ASGs requirement or creates unnecessary risk.

#### az500-d2-q14 (hard)

**Scenario:** Helix x Pulse Networks

Helix x Pulse Networks has a production issue involving Private Endpoints and Private Link. The team wants the fastest secure remediation, not a temporary workaround. What is the best answer? The solution must minimize blast radius and preserve investigation evidence.

- A. allow public network access from all networks
- B. use only an NSG on the client subnet
- C. share storage keys
- D. create Private Endpoints with private DNS integration

**Answer:** D

**Explanation:** The best answer is to create Private Endpoints with private DNS integration. This directly addresses Private Endpoints and Private Link, keeps permissions scoped, and matches the exam objective for Secure networking. In exam scenarios, prefer controls that are enforceable, auditable, and least-privileged over broad access or manual process.

**Why the others are wrong:**
- A: This does not fully meet the Private Endpoints and Private Link requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- B: This does not fully meet the Private Endpoints and Private Link requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- C: This does not fully meet the Private Endpoints and Private Link requirement or creates unnecessary risk.

#### az500-d2-q15 (medium)

**Scenario:** Nexus Financial

You are designing controls for Nexus Financial. The requirement is to centralize outbound filtering for hub-spoke networks. Which implementation is the most appropriate?

- A. route traffic through Azure Firewall and manage rules with firewall policy
- B. place NSGs only on every NIC
- C. disable UDRs
- D. use a public load balancer for egress control

**Answer:** A

**Explanation:** The best answer is to route traffic through Azure Firewall and manage rules with firewall policy. This directly addresses Azure Firewall and firewall policies, keeps permissions scoped, and matches the exam objective for Secure networking.

**Why the others are wrong:**
- B: This does not fully meet the Azure Firewall and firewall policies requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- C: This does not fully meet the Azure Firewall and firewall policies requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- D: This does not fully meet the Azure Firewall and firewall policies requirement or creates unnecessary risk.

#### az500-d2-q16 (easy)

**Scenario:** FortisAid Healthcare

FortisAid Healthcare is working in a healthcare tenant with sensitive patient data. The security lead needs to protect public web apps from common web attacks. Which action best satisfies the requirement while following least privilege?

- A. use a storage firewall
- B. enable WAF on Application Gateway or Azure Front Door with managed rules
- C. use only PIM
- D. turn off TLS inspection everywhere

**Answer:** B

**Explanation:** The best answer is to enable WAF on Application Gateway or Azure Front Door with managed rules. This directly addresses Web Application Firewall, keeps permissions scoped, and matches the exam objective for Secure networking.

**Why the others are wrong:**
- A: This does not fully meet the Web Application Firewall requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- C: This does not fully meet the Web Application Firewall requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- D: This does not fully meet the Web Application Firewall requirement or creates unnecessary risk.

- A. add more NSG deny rules only
- B. rotate storage keys
- C. enable Azure DDoS Network Protection for the virtual network
- D. create an access review

**Answer:** C

**Explanation:** The best answer is to enable Azure DDoS Network Protection for the virtual network. This directly addresses DDoS Protection, keeps permissions scoped, and matches the exam objective for Secure networking.

#### az500-d2-q45 (medium)

**Scenario:** ClearVault Finance

You are designing controls for ClearVault Finance. The requirement is to centralize outbound filtering for hub-spoke networks. Which implementation is the most appropriate?

- A. place NSGs only on every NIC
- B. disable UDRs
- C. route traffic through Azure Firewall and manage rules with firewall policy
- D. use a public load balancer for egress control

**Answer:** C

**Explanation:** The best answer is to route traffic through Azure Firewall and manage rules with firewall policy. This directly addresses Azure Firewall and firewall policies, keeps permissions scoped, and matches the exam objective for Secure networking.

**Why the others are wrong:**
- A: This does not fully meet the Azure Firewall and firewall policies requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- B: This does not fully meet the Azure Firewall and firewall policies requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- D: This does not fully meet the Azure Firewall and firewall policies requirement or creates unnecessary risk.

- B. use public IPs for databases
- C. create NSG rules using ASGs for source and destination tiers

### Secure compute, storage, and databases

#### az500-d3-q01 (easy)

**Scenario:** Helix x Pulse Networks

Helix x Pulse Networks is working in a post-acquisition identity consolidation. The security lead needs to remove public RDP/SSH exposure. Which action best satisfies the requirement while following least privilege?

- A. deploy Azure Bastion and enable JIT VM access
- B. open port 3389 to the internet
- C. share a local administrator password
- D. disable Defender for Servers

**Answer:** A

**Explanation:** The best answer is to deploy Azure Bastion and enable JIT VM access. This directly addresses VM security, Bastion, and JIT, keeps permissions scoped, and matches the exam objective for Secure compute, storage, and databases.

**Why the others are wrong:**
- B: This does not fully meet the VM security, Bastion, and JIT requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- C: This does not fully meet the VM security, Bastion, and JIT requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- D: This does not fully meet the VM security, Bastion, and JIT requirement or creates unnecessary risk.

#### az500-d3-q02 (medium)

**Scenario:** Nexus Financial

During a review at Nexus Financial, auditors found a gap related to disk encryption and trusted launch. You must fix it without adding unnecessary standing access. What should you do?

- A. rely only on NSGs
- B. use encryption at host or disk encryption plus trusted launch features where supported
- C. turn off vTPM
- D. store keys in code

**Answer:** B

**Explanation:** The best answer is to use encryption at host or disk encryption plus trusted launch features where supported. This directly addresses disk encryption and trusted launch, keeps permissions scoped, and matches the exam objective for Secure compute, storage, and databases.

**Why the others are wrong:**
- A: This does not fully meet the disk encryption and trusted launch requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- C: This does not fully meet the disk encryption and trusted launch requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- D: This does not fully meet the disk encryption and trusted launch requirement or creates unnecessary risk.

- C. disable diagnostics
- D. disable public access, use private access, RBAC, soft delete, versioning, and immutable storage as needed

This directly addresses storage account hardening, keeps permissions scoped, and matches the exam objective for Secure compute, storage, and databases. In exam scenarios, prefer controls that are enforceable, auditable, and least-privileged over broad access or manual process.

#### az500-d3-q27 (medium)

**Scenario:** FortisAid Healthcare

- B. disable auditing
- C. enable auditing, Microsoft Defender for SQL, TDE, vulnerability assessment, and private connectivity
- D. use shared SQL admin credentials

#### az500-d3-q29 (hard)

- A. deploy Azure Bastion and enable JIT VM access
- B. open port 3389 to the internet
- C. share a local administrator password
- D. disable Defender for Servers

**Explanation:** The best answer is to deploy Azure Bastion and enable JIT VM access. This directly addresses VM security, Bastion, and JIT, keeps permissions scoped, and matches the exam objective for Secure compute, storage, and databases. In exam scenarios, prefer controls that are enforceable, auditable, and least-privileged over broad access or manual process.

**Why the others are wrong:**
- B: This does not fully meet the VM security, Bastion, and JIT requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- C: This does not fully meet the VM security, Bastion, and JIT requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- D: This does not fully meet the VM security, Bastion, and JIT requirement or creates unnecessary risk.

#### az500-d4-q01 (easy)

**Scenario:** Nexus Financial

Nexus Financial is working in a regulated finance environment. The security lead needs to prioritize misconfigurations across subscriptions. Which action best satisfies the requirement while following least privilege?

- A. use only activity logs
- B. turn off Azure Policy
- C. use Defender for Cloud recommendations, secure score, and regulatory compliance
- D. grant all users Security Admin

**Answer:** C

**Explanation:** The best answer is to use Defender for Cloud recommendations, secure score, and regulatory compliance. This directly addresses Defender for Cloud posture management, keeps permissions scoped, and matches the exam objective for Secure Azure using Defender for Cloud and Sentinel.

**Why the others are wrong:**
- A: This does not fully meet the Defender for Cloud posture management requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- B: This does not fully meet the Defender for Cloud posture management requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- D: This does not fully meet the Defender for Cloud posture management requirement or creates unnecessary risk.

- A. enable only Microsoft Sentinel
- B. create an NSG rule
- C. use company branding
- D. enable the relevant Defender for Cloud plans at the subscription or workspace scope

**Answer:** D

**Explanation:** The best answer is to enable the relevant Defender for Cloud plans at the subscription or workspace scope. This directly addresses Defender workload protections, keeps permissions scoped, and matches the exam objective for Secure Azure using Defender for Cloud and Sentinel.

**Why the others are wrong:**
- A: This does not fully meet the Defender workload protections requirement or creates unnecessary risk.

#### az500-d4-q09 (hard)

**Scenario:** Nexus Financial

Nexus Financial has a production issue involving Sentinel data connectors. The team wants the fastest secure remediation, not a temporary workaround. What is the best answer? The solution must minimize blast radius and preserve investigation evidence.

- A. create a workbook without data
- B. disable diagnostic settings
- C. configure Microsoft Sentinel data connectors for the required sources
- D. export CSV files manually

**Answer:** C

**Explanation:** The best answer is to configure Microsoft Sentinel data connectors for the required sources. This directly addresses Sentinel data connectors, keeps permissions scoped, and matches the exam objective for Secure Azure using Defender for Cloud and Sentinel. In exam scenarios, prefer controls that are enforceable, auditable, and least-privileged over broad access or manual process.

**Why the others are wrong:**
- A: This does not fully meet the Sentinel data connectors requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- B: This does not fully meet the Sentinel data connectors requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- D: This does not fully meet the Sentinel data connectors requirement or creates unnecessary risk.

#### az500-d4-q10 (medium)

**Scenario:** FortisAid Healthcare

You are designing controls for FortisAid Healthcare. The requirement is to detect brute force, impossible travel, and suspicious admin activity. Which implementation is the most appropriate?

- A. use only a dashboard
- B. rename the workspace
- C. create an access package
- D. create scheduled analytics rules with KQL and entity mapping

**Answer:** D

**Explanation:** The best answer is to create scheduled analytics rules with KQL and entity mapping. This directly addresses KQL analytics rules, keeps permissions scoped, and matches the exam objective for Secure Azure using Defender for Cloud and Sentinel.

**Why the others are wrong:**
- A: This does not fully meet the KQL analytics rules requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- B: This does not fully meet the KQL analytics rules requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- C: This does not fully meet the KQL analytics rules requirement or creates unnecessary risk.

#### az500-d4-q11 (easy)

- A. create automation rules and Logic App playbooks
- B. manually email screenshots
- C. disable incident creation
- D. use a storage lifecycle rule

**Answer:** A

**Explanation:** The best answer is to create automation rules and Logic App playbooks. This directly addresses Sentinel automation and playbooks, keeps permissions scoped, and matches the exam objective for Secure Azure using Defender for Cloud and Sentinel.

**Why the others are wrong:**

#### az500-d4-q12 (medium)

**Scenario:** Helix x Pulse Networks

During a review at Helix x Pulse Networks, auditors found a gap related to AMA and DCR telemetry. You must fix it without adding unnecessary standing access. What should you do?

- A. install deprecated agents everywhere
- B. deploy Azure Monitor Agent with Data Collection Rules
- C. collect no logs to reduce noise
- D. store logs in Key Vault

**Answer:** B

**Explanation:** The best answer is to deploy Azure Monitor Agent with Data Collection Rules. This directly addresses AMA and DCR telemetry, keeps permissions scoped, and matches the exam objective for Secure Azure using Defender for Cloud and Sentinel.

**Why the others are wrong:**
- A: This does not fully meet the AMA and DCR telemetry requirement or creates unnecessary risk.

- D: This does not fully meet the AMA and DCR telemetry requirement or creates unnecessary risk.

#### az500-d4-q13 (medium)

**Scenario:** Nexus Financial

A change request at Nexus Financial says: "prioritize misconfigurations across subscriptions." The solution must be auditable and aligned to Microsoft cloud security practices. Which option should you choose?

- A. use only activity logs
- B. turn off Azure Policy
- C. use Defender for Cloud recommendations, secure score, and regulatory compliance
- D. grant all users Security Admin

**Answer:** C

**Explanation:** The best answer is to use Defender for Cloud recommendations, secure score, and regulatory compliance. This directly addresses Defender for Cloud posture management, keeps permissions scoped, and matches the exam objective for Secure Azure using Defender for Cloud and Sentinel.

**Why the others are wrong:**
- A: This does not fully meet the Defender for Cloud posture management requirement or creates unnecessary risk.

#### az500-d4-q14 (hard)

**Scenario:** FortisAid Healthcare

FortisAid Healthcare has a production issue involving Defender workload protections. The team wants the fastest secure remediation, not a temporary workaround. What is the best answer? The solution must minimize blast radius and preserve investigation evidence.

- A. enable only Microsoft Sentinel
- B. create an NSG rule
- C. use company branding
- D. enable the relevant Defender for Cloud plans at the subscription or workspace scope

**Answer:** D

**Explanation:** The best answer is to enable the relevant Defender for Cloud plans at the subscription or workspace scope. This directly addresses Defender workload protections, keeps permissions scoped, and matches the exam objective for Secure Azure using Defender for Cloud and Sentinel. In exam scenarios, prefer controls that are enforceable, auditable, and least-privileged over broad access or manual process.

**Why the others are wrong:**

#### az500-d4-q42 (medium)

**Scenario:** FortisAid Healthcare

During a review at FortisAid Healthcare, auditors found a gap related to AMA and DCR telemetry. You must fix it without adding unnecessary standing access. What should you do?

- A. install deprecated agents everywhere
- B. collect no logs to reduce noise
- C. store logs in Key Vault
- D. deploy Azure Monitor Agent with Data Collection Rules

**Answer:** D

**Explanation:** The best answer is to deploy Azure Monitor Agent with Data Collection Rules. This directly addresses AMA and DCR telemetry, keeps permissions scoped, and matches the exam objective for Secure Azure using Defender for Cloud and Sentinel.

**Why the others are wrong:**
- A: This does not fully meet the AMA and DCR telemetry requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- B: This does not fully meet the AMA and DCR telemetry requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- C: This does not fully meet the AMA and DCR telemetry requirement or creates unnecessary risk.

#### az500-d4-q43 (medium)

- A. use Defender for Cloud recommendations, secure score, and regulatory compliance
- B. use only activity logs
- C. turn off Azure Policy
- D. grant all users Security Admin

#### az500-d4-q44 (hard)

**Scenario:** Helix x Pulse Networks

Helix x Pulse Networks has a production issue involving Defender workload protections. The team wants the fastest secure remediation, not a temporary workaround. What is the best answer? The solution must minimize blast radius and preserve investigation evidence.

- A. enable only Microsoft Sentinel
- B. enable the relevant Defender for Cloud plans at the subscription or workspace scope
- C. create an NSG rule
- D. use company branding

**Answer:** B

**Explanation:** The best answer is to enable the relevant Defender for Cloud plans at the subscription or workspace scope. This directly addresses Defender workload protections, keeps permissions scoped, and matches the exam objective for Secure Azure using Defender for Cloud and Sentinel. In exam scenarios, prefer controls that are enforceable, auditable, and least-privileged over broad access or manual process.

**Why the others are wrong:**
- A: This does not fully meet the Defender workload protections requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- C: This does not fully meet the Defender workload protections requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
- D: This does not fully meet the Defender workload protections requirement or creates unnecessary risk.
